## Starting context: `neither_subj-det`
- time stamp: `Tue Aug  3 22:33:53 EDT 2021`
- data directory: `data/neg-ext-subj/Nyt2.neither_subj-det`
- hits table: `hits/neg-ext-subj/Nyt2_neither_subj-det`
```{js}
pattern{
  ADV [xpos=RB,  lemma <> "not"|"hardly"|"scarcely"|"never"|"rarely"|"barely"|"seldom"|"no"];
  ADJ [xpos=JJ]; 
  BE [lemma="be"];
  ADV < ADJ;
  mod: ADJ -[advmod]-> ADV;
  cop: ADJ -[cop]-> BE;
  N [lemma="neither"]; 
  S [];
  det: S -[det]-> N; 
  sub: ADJ -[nsubj|nsubjpass]-> S;
  S << BE
}
```

## Starting context: `no-one_subj-NP`
- time stamp: `Wed Aug  4 06:15:12 EDT 2021`
- data directory: `data/neg-ext-subj/Nyt2.no-one_subj-NP`
- hits table: `hits/neg-ext-subj/Nyt2_no-one_subj-NP`
```{js}
pattern {
  ADV [xpos=RB,  lemma <> "not"|"hardly"|"scarcely"|"never"|"rarely"|"barely"|"seldom"|"no"];
  ADJ [xpos=JJ]; 
  BE [lemma="be"];
  ADV < ADJ;
  mod: ADJ -[advmod]-> ADV;
  cop: ADJ -[cop]-> BE;
  S [lemma="one"]; 
  N [lemma="no"];
  det: S -[det]-> N;
  sub: ADJ -[nsubj|nsubjpass]-> S;
  S << BE
}
```  

## Starting context: `no_subj-det`
- time stamp: `Wed Aug  4 14:12:26 EDT 2021`
- data directory: `data/neg-ext-subj/Nyt2.no_subj-det`
- hits table: `hits/neg-ext-subj/Nyt2_no_subj-det`
```{js}
pattern {
  ADV [xpos=RB,  lemma <> "not"|"hardly"|"scarcely"|"never"|"rarely"|"barely"|"seldom"|"no"];
  ADJ [xpos=JJ]; 
  BE [lemma="be"];
  ADV < ADJ;
  mod: ADJ -[advmod]-> ADV;
  cop: ADJ -[cop]-> BE;
  S [lemma <> "one"]; 
  N [lemma="no"];
  det: S -[det]-> N;
  sub: ADJ -[nsubj|nsubjpass]-> S;
  S << BE
}
```  
